            </ul>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </li>

              </p>

Kitchen offers a nice size breakfast area along with center island. The kitchen overlooks the family room with wood burning fireplace. The second floor offers 5 spacious bedrooms and 3 full updated baths

Property offers EXTENSIVE hard and landscaping in the front and back of the home including stone pavers, heated in ground pool, shed and a private backyard setting backing to space and not other homes!           <h2 class="zsg-separator">
